      (0): Linear(in_features=1536, out_features=256, bias=True)
      (1): LayerNorm((256,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (2): ReLU(inplace=True)
    )
    (agent_level_embedding_layer): Sequential(
      (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=512, bias=True)
      (1): ReLU()
      (2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=256, bias=True)
    )
    (scene_level_ego_embedding_layer): Sequential(
      (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=512, bias=True)
      (1): ReLU()
      (2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=256, bias=True)
    )
    (scene_level_offset_embedding_layer): Sequential(
      (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=512, bias=True)
      (1): ReLU()
      (2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=256, bias=True)
    )
    (boxes_query_embedding_layer): Sequential(
      (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=512, bias=True)
      (1): ReLU()
      (2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=256, bias=True)
    )
    (traj_cls_branches): ModuleList(
      (0-2): 3 x Sequential(
        (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
        (1): LayerNorm((256,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (2): ReLU(inplace=True)
        (3): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
        (4): LayerNorm((256,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (5): ReLU(inplace=True)
        (6): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=1, bias=True)
      )
    )
    (traj_reg_branches): ModuleList(
      (0-2): 3 x Sequential(
        (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
        (1): ReLU()
        (2): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
        (3): ReLU()
        (4): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=60, bias=True)
      )
    )
  )
  (planning_head): DiffusionPlanningHead(
    (bev_track_bridge): BEVToContextBridge(
      (bev_compress): Sequential(
        (0): Conv2d(256, 256, kernel_size=(5, 5), stride=(5, 5))
        (1): ReLU()
        (2): Conv2d(256, 256, kernel_size=(5, 5), stride=(5, 5))
        (3): ReLU()
      )
      (track_proj): Sequential(
        (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
        (1): LayerNorm((256,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      )
      (agent_encoder): TransformerEncoder(
        (layers): ModuleList(
          (0): TransformerEncoderLayer(
            (self_attn): MultiheadAttention(
              (out_proj): NonDynamicallyQuantizableLinear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
            )
            (linear1): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
            (dropout): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
            (linear2): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
            (norm1): LayerNorm((256,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
            (norm2): LayerNorm((256,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
            (dropout1): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
            (dropout2): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
          )
        )
      )
    )
    (ego_bridge): EgoContextBridge(
      (ego_fuser): Sequential(
        (0): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=256, bias=True)
        (1): LayerNorm((256,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (2): GELU(approximate='none')
      )
      (command_embed): Embedding(3, 256)
      (routing_fuser): Sequential(
        (0): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=256, bias=True)
        (1): LayerNorm((256,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (2): GELU(approximate='none')
      )
    )
    (t_embedder): TimestepEmbedder(
      (mlp): Sequential(
        (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
        (1): SiLU()
        (2): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
      )
    )
    (ego_time_pe): SinusoidalPE()
    (preproj): MLP2(
      (fc1): Linear(in_features=2, out_features=256, bias=True)
      (act): GELU(approximate='none')
      (norm): RMSNorm()
      (fc2): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
    )
    (vector_in): MLP2(
      (fc1): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
      (act): GELU(approximate='none')
      (norm): RMSNorm()
      (fc2): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
    )
    (routing_in): MLP2(
      (fc1): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
      (act): GELU(approximate='none')
      (norm): RMSNorm()
      (fc2): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
    )
    (context_in): MLP2(
      (fc1): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
      (act): GELU(approximate='none')
      (norm): RMSNorm()
      (fc2): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
    )
    (dit_blocks): ModuleList(
      (0-1): 2 x DiTBlock(
        (norm1): LayerNorm((256,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=False)
        (norm2): LayerNorm((256,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=False)
        (norm3): LayerNorm((256,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=False)
        (self_attn): MultiheadAttention(
          (out_proj): NonDynamicallyQuantizableLinear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
        )
        (cross_attn): MultiheadAttention(
          (out_proj): NonDynamicallyQuantizableLinear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
        )
        (ffn): Sequential(
          (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (1): GELU(approximate='none')
          (2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=256, bias=True)
        )
        (adaLN_modulation): Sequential(
          (0): SiLU()
          (1): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=1536, bias=True)
        )
      )
    )
    (final_layer): FinalLayer(
      (norm): LayerNorm((256,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=False)
      (linear): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=2, bias=True)
      (adaLN_modulation): Sequential(
        (0): SiLU()
        (1): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=512, bias=True)
      )
    )
    (loss_collision): ModuleList()
  )
)
